1561234752309</date>
<rate>5< /rate>< review>
I love this place! It's a local, quick stop joint for lunches on busy workdays. Prices are low for the area. Cash only, there's an atm onsite. Decent amount of tables indoors and two tables outdoors. Dog friendly outside. Owners and employees are wonderful, attentive, and friendly. A great place to become a regular at. Sandwiches are good, banh mi is great, Vietnamese specials (noodles, rice, pho) are simple/average, food is consistent in quality. Nothing amazing, ground breaking, or foodie/hipster/experimental/gastro/expensive about this place. It's a simple, quick, affordable place near many office locations with awesome staff and consistent food.</review>

<text>These folks are great!  Consistent quality on sandwiches.
Friendly service.    Convenient location for people that work in the general area.  (I recommend calling in your order in advance if you have limited lunch  break time)

Good price (especially given other nearby food options).  But remember: CASH ONLY... although they do have an ATM onsite if needed.

The PHO is great! I order it at least 1-2 times per week. Definitely my favorite thing on the menu aside from the Bahn Mi Sandwiches.
They also have some alright breakfast options.

All in all, you can't go wrong with this cool little hole in the wall.<//text>< time>

< Text>
Had never been before, would go back in an instant. Found on Google, didn't know what to expect. Amazing! Very sweet ladies asked if it was our first time and proceeded to give us the star treatment. They went over all of the ice cream choices and let us sample whatever we wanted. Then went over the menu. We had the churro dessert with banana graham cracker and fresh strawberry ice creams. The Mexican hot chocolate ice cream and rum raisin ice cream was a favorite. The best churros we have ever tasted, small bites, perfectly crisp and hot. In store made hot fudge was to die for and the atmosphere was great. Will go back for sure. Ice cream tasted like it was freshly churned and creamy and smooth all the way through. No ice crystals like you get at some places. Great place for dessert!</Text>

< Text>
The juice is definitely worth the squeeze on this one! It is not a very far or difficult walk. There is a consistent elevation game and there is one necessary river crossing, but these should not stop you. If there is a ton of water it may be difficult to cross the river, but today the skipping stones that are to hop across the river, or completely dry. There was a little bit of water at the bottom. The falls was not extremely glorious with rushing water, but it is still a beautiful land feature. This is great hike for people who don't want to go on a very long hike and who can make a moderate hike</Text>

< review>
This trail is a beautiful hiking spot which takes you to the top of a tall waterfall which can overlook the entire trail. There are some dangerous ledges, and their is wildlife in the area which includes Mountain Lions, so be sure to take all proper percussion. All in all a great trail for the outdoorsy!</review>

<user>115542738258111779553<//user><user_name>Dwight James<//user_name>< Date>
1524457138631</Date>
<Rate>5< /Rate><Text>Beautiful! Great place!
To use the parking area you need an Adventure Pass. This is 4.5 mile hike in (9 round trip) from the trailhead to the falls. The path itself is single walker wide with with a good bit of elevation change. There are areas where a slip could cause a fall of several hundred feet and surly, mortality. And, areas with less extreme but certainly potentially fatal falls could occur. Please beware with small children! The path itself is mostly not difficult to navigate though there are a few areas where you are going to need to be able walk across 100% rocky areas. And be prepared for large rocks all along the path. You will need to be aware. As well, there is the potential for Mountain Lions and Rattlesnake so, take appropriate precautions. When we went, we passed 5 or 6 other parties so, it's not completely unknown. Still, most wouldn't want to try and navigate this area in the dark and there is no cellular service.<//Text><pictures>None<//pictures>< resp>
None</resp>

< Review>
This is one of the best taquirea in SF. It's far away from mission so that means less tourist come through here. Mainly SF natives know about this spot. Everything is fresh and flavorful. Tucked away in one of the worst crime ridden parts of SF, between Bayview and Visitation valley they've recently identified this area as Portola to make this area "seem" nicer and more welcoming. Coming to this part of the city ain't for the faint of heart I've seen fist fights, break ins, hit and runs, and occasionally hear shootings but this is where I grew up so it's all g for me. But I sure hope this review detours all tourist from coming here cause Id hate to stand in a long line for my super shrimp and steak burrito /refried beans on the side, which is the absolute best and must have. I'm a picky guy in terms of food, el farlito is about a 6 out of 10 the place across the street from them la Guadalajara is 6.5 out of 10 Cinco de mayo is of course 10 out of 10. They just killing it here just like the hood in which it resides. You want a killer burrito you come here. If you want 10 out of 10 taco you go to la taquirea.</Review>

Their tacos are great... and that means a lot here in Madera! There are so many taco trucks out there but honestly I believe they're mostly on the mediocre side of taco making industry. Cachanilla stands out from the rest! Their salsas are right on point, their meat is flavorful, they puts tons of veggies on each taco and they put cabbage on the tacos instead of lettuce and that to me is a winner on it's own. Don't miss the chance to try them. It's well worth the long line.<//review>
